Wir entwickeln für Sie verkaufsstarke Marketing- und Vertriebskonzepte, strategische Vorteilsargumentationen für Handelspartner und Investoren, medienübergreifende online und offline Kampagnen.
                 <br/>
                 Auf Basis jahrzehntelanger Werbe- und Medienerfahrung entdecken wir mit Ihnen gemeinsam neue Lösungswege und spannende Nischen für Ihre Geschäftsentwicklung. Lassen Sie sich auf eine neue kreative Sicht der Dinge ein, die Ihr Unternehmen weiterbringt und die Ihnen neue interessante Perspektiven eröffnet. Sprechen Sie mit uns!

Voraussetzung ist eine evidenzbasierte Unternehmensführung, die an Hand von generierten Daten und Testergebnissen eine präzise Dimensionierung und Platzierung von Budget- und Personalressourcen passend zu den angestrebten Zielen ermöglicht.

               <div class="grve-element grve-image markenwebsite grve-align-center" style="">
                <img alt="" class="attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail" data-attachment-id="25341" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="markenwebsite-label" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?fit=439%2C437&amp;ssl=1" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?fit=300%2C300&amp;ssl=1" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?fit=439%2C437&amp;ssl=1" data-orig-size="439,437" data-permalink="https://www.effektor.de/intro/markenwebsite-label/" height="150" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" src="https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?resize=150%2C150&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?w=439&amp;ssl=1 439w, https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?resize=150%2C150&amp;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/markenwebsite-label.png?resize=300%2C300&amp;ssl=1 300w" width="150"/>

               <div class="grve-element grve-text">
                <div id="abovecontainer">
                 <img data-recalc-dims="1" src="https://i0.wp.com/www.effektor.de/wp-content/uploads/2017/08/brains.png?w=1080&amp;ssl=1" style="position: absolute; width: 330px !important; height: auto; z-index: 1; bottom: -380px; left: 200px;"/>

                <div id="container">
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="wpb_raw_code wpb_raw_js">
                <div class="wpb_wrapper">
                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  // ----------------------------------------
         // Particle
         // ----------------------------------------
 
         function Particle( x, y, radius ) {
             this.init( x, y, radius );
         }
 
         Particle.prototype = {
 
             init: function( x, y, radius ) {
 
                 this.alive = true;
 
                 this.radius = radius || 10;
                 this.wander = 0.15;
                 this.theta = random( TWO_PI );
                 this.drag = 0.92;
                 this.color = '#8a52c4';
 
                 this.x = x || 0.0;
                 this.y = y || 0.0;
 
                 this.vx = 0.0;
                 this.vy = 0.0;
             },
 
             move: function() {
 
                 this.x += this.vx;
                 this.y += this.vy;
 
                 this.vx *= this.drag;
                 this.vy *= this.drag;
 
                 this.theta += random( -0.5, 0.5 ) * this.wander;
                 this.vx += sin( this.theta ) * 0.1;
                 this.vy += cos( this.theta ) * 0.1;
 
                 this.radius *= 0.96;
                 this.alive = this.radius > 0.5;
             },
 
             draw: function( ctx ) {
 
                 ctx.beginPath();
                 ctx.arc( this.x, this.y, this.radius, 0, TWO_PI );
                 ctx.fillStyle = this.color;
                 ctx.fill();
             }
         };
 
         // ----------------------------------------
         // Example
         // ----------------------------------------
      
 var MAX_PARTICLES = 280;
         var COLOURS = [ '#fc7f2b', '#8a52c4', '#801ac1', '#F38630', '#FA6900', '#FF4E50', '#F9D423' ];
 
         var particles = [];
         var pool = [];
 
         var demo = Sketch.create({
             container: document.getElementById( 'container' ),
             retina: 'auto'
         });
 
         demo.setup = function() {
 
             // Set off some initial particles.
             var i, x, y;
 
             for ( i = 0; i < 20; i++ ) {
                 x = ( demo.width * 0.5 ) + random( -100, 100 );
                 y = ( demo.height * 0.5 ) + random( -100, 100 );
                 demo.spawn( x, y );
             }
         };
 
         demo.spawn = function( x, y ) {
             
             var particle, theta, force;
 
             if ( particles.length >= MAX_PARTICLES )
                 pool.push( particles.shift() );
 
             particle = pool.length ? pool.pop() : new Particle();
             particle.init( x, y, random( 5, 40 ) );
 
             particle.wander = random( 0.5, 2.0 );
             particle.color = random( COLOURS );
             particle.drag = random( 0.9, 0.99 );
 
             theta = random( TWO_PI );
             force = random( 2, 8 );
 
             particle.vx = sin( theta ) * force;
             particle.vy = cos( theta ) * force;
 
             particles.push( particle );
         };
 
         demo.update = function() {
 
             var i, particle;
 
             for ( i = particles.length - 1; i >= 0; i-- ) {
 
                 particle = particles[i];
 
                 if ( particle.alive ) particle.move();
                 else pool.push( particles.splice( i, 1 )[0] );
             }
         };
 
         demo.draw = function() {
 
             demo.globalCompositeOperation  = 'lighter';
 
             for ( var i = particles.length - 1; i >= 0; i-- ) {
                 particles[i].draw( demo );
             }
         };
 
         demo.mousemove = function() {
 
             var particle, theta, force, touch, max, i, j, n;
 
             for ( i = 0, n = demo.touches.length; i < n; i++ ) {
 
                 touch = demo.touches[i], max = random( 1, 4 );
                 for ( j = 0; j < max; j++ ) {
                   demo.spawn( touch.x, touch.y );
                 }
 
             }
         };
                 </script>
                </div>
               </div>

    function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
 				var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";
 				errorMessage += "<br> This includes make eliminates the revolution slider libraries, and make it not work.";
 				errorMessage += "<br><br> To fix it you can:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. In the Slider Settings -> Troubleshooting set option:  <strong><b>Put JS Includes To Body</b></strong> option to true.";
 				errorMessage += "<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2. Find the double jquery.js include and remove it.";
 				errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
 					jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);
 			}

    var screen_width = Math.max( screen.width, screen.height );var devicePixelRatio = window.devicePixelRatio ? window.devicePixelRatio : 1;document.cookie = 'resolution=' + screen_width + ',' + devicePixelRatio + '; path=/';
 jQuery(document).ready(function() {
   //variable for the 'stroke-dashoffset' unit
   var $dashOffset = jQuery(".path").css("stroke-dashoffset");
   //on a scroll event - execute function
   jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
     //calculate how far down the page the user is 
     var $percentageComplete = ((jQuery(window).scrollTop() / (jQuery("html").height() - jQuery(window).height())) * 100);
     //convert dashoffset pixel value to interger
     var $newUnit = parseInt($dashOffset, 10);
     //get the value to be subtracted from the 'stroke-dashoffset'
     var $offsetUnit = $percentageComplete * ($newUnit / 100);
     //set the new value of the dashoffset to create the drawing effect
     jQuery(".path").css("stroke-dashoffset", $newUnit - $offsetUnit);
   });
 });
   </script>
